ANSWER:PERSEUS BONUS:Perseus’ mother, Danae, was thrown into a tower by her father so that she would not bear a child. What was her father’s name? ANSWER:ACRISIUS BONUS:Acrisius did this to prevent the prophecy of his death being fulfilled. But Fate cannot be escaped. With what did Perseus fulfill the prophecy? ANSWER:WITH A DISCUS (PERSEUS KILLED ACRISIUS IN A COMPETITION BY ACCIDENT) 
In Book I of the Iliad, what enraged Greek chieftain nearly kills Agamemnon, but is literally held back by the goddess Athena? ANSWER:ACHILLES BONUS:Achilles’ anger was justified. Agamemnon was planning to take Achilles’ girl after he had lost his girl. Who was Achilles’ girl? ANSWER:BRISEIS BONUS:What course of action does Achilles take after his argument with Agamemnon? ANSWER:HE WITHDRAWS FROM THE WAR/FIGHTING 
What man, whose fate was tied to the condition of a log, fell in love with the huntress Atalanta? ANSWER:MELEAGER BONUS:Who was Meleager’s mother, who threw the log into the fire, ending her son’s life? ANSWER:ALTHAEA BONUS: Why had Althaea ended Meleager’s life? ANSWER:HE KILLED HER BROTHERS/HIS UNCLES 
To whom did the bloodied ghost of Sychaeus appear, recounting his death by her own brother and telling this Phoenician woman to flee? ANSWER:DIDO BONUS: Name Dido’s brother, who assassinated Sychaeus. ANSWER:PYGMALION BONUS:Dido founded what city, which is beloved to Juno? ANSWER:CARTHAGE 
Which “leader” of Penelope’s suitors was the first to speak and and first to die? ANSWER:ANTINOUS BONUS:One of the suitors insults the disguised Odysseus and challenges him to a boxing match. What goddess helps Odysseus by giving him extra strength? ANSWER:ATHENA BONUS: To prove her husband’s identity, Penelope asked Odysseus to move their bed. He correctly responded that the bed was impossible to move. Why couldn’t the bed be moved? ANSWER:PART OF THE BED IS A TREE 
While performing one of his labors, Hercules stops at the house of his old friend Admetus [AD-MEET-TUS]. What wife of Admetus died? ANSWER:ALCESTIS BONUS:Who had warned Admetus that he would die soon unless he found a substitute? ANSWER:APOLLO BONUS: In an attempt to redeem himself, Hercules wrestles with what god of death for Alcestis’ shadow. ANSWER:THANATOS 
Who am I? I am the son of Maia and Jupiter. After I was born, I made off with Apollo’s cattle and created a lyre with a turtle shell. ANSWER:MERCURY BONUS: What mortal did Mercury turn into stone for betraying him to Apollo? ANSWER:BATTUS BONUS:Mercury was found out by Apollo quickly. What did Mercury give Apollo which quelled his anger? ANSWER:THE LYRE 
Picus, Glaucus and Odysseus were all loved by what sorceress, daughter of Helios? ANSWER:CIRCE BONUS:Only one of these men reciprocated Circe’s affections. Who was he? ANSWER:ODYSSEUS BONUS:Glaucus loved another woman. Name the woman he loved. ANSWER:SCYLLA 
Snakes are scary, right? I remember two snakes came out of the sea and killed a Trojan man who insisted the Trojan Horse should not be brought into the walls of Troy. What was his name again? ANSWER:LAOCOON BONUS:What other Trojan knew the Trojan Horse was a bad idea, but as usual, was not heeded because of a curse from Apollo? ANSWER:CASSANDRA BONUS:What Greek convinced the Trojans into bringing the horse into the city? ANSWER:SINON 
What titular character is punished by her uncle for attempting to bury her brother, Polynices? ANSWER:ANTIGONE BONUS:Who, Antigone’s own relative, had forbidden Polynices’ burial? ANSWER:CREON BONUS:What was Antigone’s punishment for violating Creon’s decree? ANSWER:SHE WAS BURIED ALIVE [PROMPT ON “DEATH”] 
After stopping in Thrace, where did the Trojans first settle because Anchises believed the place was their destined motherland? ANSWER:CRETE BONUS:After a year the Trojans settled Crete, they soon find out this was the wrong place. What is the biggest natural indicator? ANSWER:A PLAGUE BONUS:What ancestor was Anchises thinking of when he thought Crete was their motherland? ANSWER:TEUCER 
What bandit, at the Isthmus of Corinth, liked to tear apart his victims with pine trees and was also known as Pityokamptes {PIT-tee-oh-CAMP-tees]? ANSWER:SINIS BONUS:What does Pityokamptes mean? ANSWER:PINE BENDER BONUS:Theseus encountered what other brigand who fed his victims to a giant turtle? ANSWER:SCYRON 
What Thracian king cut out his sister-in-law’s tongue and hid her in a shack while he told his wife that her sister had died on the journey from Athens? ANSWER:TEREUS BONUS:Who was Tereus’ wife, who only learned of Tereus’ crime when Philomela, her sister sent a weaving detailing what happened? ANSWER:PROCNE BONUS:Procne in revenge decides to kill their son and feed him to an unsuspecting Tereus. What is the son’s name? ANSWER:ITYS [IH-TUS] 
Who in the Underworld was punished for feeding mortal flesh to the gods and stands in a pool of water grasping for low-hanging fruits? ANSWER:TANTALUS BONUS:Who in the Underworld is bound on constantly-turning, fiery wheel? ANSWER:IXION BONUS:Who in the Underworld is cursed to roll a rock up a hill for eternity, never reaching the top? ANSWER:SISYPHUS 
Juno transformed herself into the elderly Beroe in order to trick what lover of Jupiter into revealing the god’s true form? ANSWER:SEMELE BONUS: After Semele’s death, from what part of Jupiter’s body was Bacchus reborn? ANSWER:THIGH BONUS:In what form did Zeus seduce Semele? ANSWER:EAGLE 
Translate this sentence from Latin to English: Circum agros meos duas horas curram. ANSWER:I WILL RUN (FOR) TWO HOURS AROUND MY FIELDS. BONUS:Translate this sentence into English: Quod aurea mala volebat, Atalanta sine magna celeritate currebat. BECAUSE SHE WANTED THE GOLDEN APPLES, ANSWER:ATALANTA RAN WITHOUT GREAT SPEED. BONUS: Now translate this sentence: Quod eum interficere voluit, Achilles cum hasta ad Hectorem cucurrit. ANSWER:BECAUSE HE WANTED TO KILL HIM, ACHILLES RAN TO(WARDS) HECTOR WITH A SPEAR. 
What two Argonauts chased away the harpies from the seer Phineus? ANSWER:ZETES AND CALAIS BONUS:What advice did Phineus give to the Argonauts? ANSWER:SEND A DOVE THROUGH THE CLASHING ROCKS [PROMPT ON “BIRD”] BONUS:What is the name of the clashing rocks? ANSWER:SYMPLEGADES 
Eileithyia [EH-LEH-THAY-UH], the goddess of childbirth, and Hebe, goddess of youth, were the daughters of what pair? ANSWER:ZEUS AND HERA BONUS: Hebe in addition was the cupbearer of the gods, but she was replaced by a Trojan prince. What was his name? ANSWER:GANYMEDE BONUS:Ganymede was the son of Tros, who was saddened by his son’s disappearance. In return, Zeus gave what to Tros? HORSES ANSWER:NOVICE 
Lucina, goddess of childbirth, was tricked by what nurse who cried, “It’s a boy!”, allowing Alcmene to finally give birth to Hercules? ANSWER:GALANTHIS BONUS: For her trick to work, what did Galanthis need the goddess of childbirth to do? ANSWER:UNTIE/UNBIND/UNCROSS HER LIMBS BONUS:Angered by her trick, into what did Lucina transform Galanthis? ANSWER:WEASEL 
What son of Iapetus stole fire concealed in a fennel stalk from Zeus who had been coveting it? ANSWER:PROMETHEUS BONUS: For this trick, how was Prometheus punished? ANSWER:HE WAS TIED TO A MOUNTAIN, HAVE HIS LIVER EATEN BY AN EAGLE EVERYDAY BONUS: To what mountain was Prometheus chained? ANSWER:CAUCASUS 
What handsome youth, the son of Myrrha, was beloved to Venus but was tragically gored by a boar? ANSWER:ADONIS BONUS:What other goddess adored Adonis so much that she and Venus quarreled over him? Jupiter had to settle the argument by saying the boy would spend one part of the year with Venus and the other with this goddess. ANSWER:PROSERPINA BONUS:Into what was the dead Adonis transformed? ANSWER:ANEMONE 
What maiden did the Trojan prince Paris abandon to seek the most beautiful woman Helen? ANSWER:OENONE BONUS: Who is the beautiful Helen’s mortal father? ANSWER:TYNDAREUS BONUS:What oath did Tyndareus make Helen’s suitors take? ANSWER:THEY WOULD ALL DEFEND THE EVENTUAL HUSBAND OF HELEN
